< text>
Okay I'm shocked this doesn't have AT LEAST a 4.7 so I had to leave a review. It should be closer to 4.9- Absolutely the best vegan sushi I have ever had!! I've tried a whole handful of vegan sushi spots including Now Sushi in Mission Bay and Kensho in OC. The Yasai is super creative in their usage of veggies and fungi rather than relying heavily on imitation seafood and that is what sets it apart. The prices are reasonable for what it is, the decor and ambiance is wonderful, and the service was EXCELLENT. Go asap!!!! (I was too excited to eat the subsequent rolls I ordered so this was the only one that got photographed.)<//text>

<Text>Great food but terrible customer service. Their poor customer service seems to be a common theme upon their poor reviews.
Everything we ate was great and I would highly recommend the brussel sprouts. The reason I did not rate this restaurant higher was due to issues with the manager.
The night we went the restaurant was busy and the service was pretty slow, which was understandable,  but what really bothered us was the unprofessional way they handled forgetting one of our orders. After waiting a while for our food and then finishing our meal, the waitress brought our check and I pointed out that we never got one of our orders which was fine, we just wanted it reduced from our bill. At this time our meal was over and it was time for us to move on with our night. She was understanding and removed it but then 3 minutes later as we were about to leave, she told us that the manager is requiring us to pay for the roll and will bring it to us. We would have gladly taken the roll earlier but at this time we were done with dinner and expressed our feelings that since this was not brought to us at the appropriate time we no longer wanted the roll.
This is a common mistake that happens with restaurants but not once has a  restaurant required us to pay for the meal after we already finished our time there and paid our bill.  After asking to speak to the manager, the waitress informed us that the manager would not come out to talk to us.  We were then guilted into paying for the roll as the waitress appeared very concerned about getting in trouble if we did not take it.

This restaurant would be great but needs a new manager!
I would have came back here again if it weren't for the issues with the manager which appears to happen frequently as stated in other reviews.< /Text>< pics>

<text>I had the worst dining experience in my life tonight due to an extremely defensive and rude hostess.  I made it a point of mine to regularly order takeout and patronize the Yasai to do my part to support local business, especially plant-based restaurants, which are going through a rough time during COVID. I even celebrated my 37th birthday here in November and my waiter was nice enough to store my birthday cake in their refrigerator. In all, I would estimate that I've patronized this restaurant roughly 20+ times. However, today was unlike any other time that I tried to order food. My date and I arrived at 6:30 PM at the Yasai on India Street and asked for a table for 2. For instance, the inside of the restaurant was full, which is a violation of COVID restrictions. Nevertheless, the outside only had one table occupied with the other 6 or so others open. The hostess said, "We don't have any seating available." I then asked how many reservations were booked and whether there was an opening soon. The hostess said, "We have an opening at 7:30." I then asked, "It's 6:30 now. Did anyone no show because there's seven seats available based on the tables." She said, "We can't be congested due to COVID." I then said, "Aren't the tables outside already socially distanced?" Then my date said, "We'll take the 7:30 time slot." The hostess then said, "Actually, we have the right to deny service. You can eat elsewhere. Have a good night!" I then asked if I could speak to the manager. Then she walked away. She comes back about 2 mins later and says, "My manager is unavailable." I said I'll wait. She then leaves again to go to the kitchen in the back of the restaurant where I can see her talking to a chef in a white hat. The hostess then returns to us in the front and says, "My manager said I'm the supervisor." I then said, "So now you're the manager or are you the supervisor? How do you supervise yourself? My date then asks her what her name is. The hostess says, "I don't have to tell you my name." Then walks away yet again! At this point it was apparent to me that the staff here provided no information to the public nor was there any visible food licensing permits, legible COVID reopen plan, or business permits. In short, there is no point of contact name or contact information displayed for patrons to even report complaints such as this, so the hostess refusing to even provide her name and her failure to bring a manager to hear my concerns is apparently business as usual. Therefore, I will never spend another dime here and encourage you to do the same.<//text><pics>None< /pics>< response>

< Text>
I was excited to try this place and went there with my wife and mother. My mother ordered a ramen, while my wife and I ordered 3 rolls to share. My mother's ramen came out in about 5 minutes, and was pretty good...all down hill from there. We proceeded to sit in the near empty restaurant for over an hour for our rolls to arrive, even though we were at one point the only ones in the restaurant.

When we asked our server about the long wait we were told that there were many to go orders to be made and only one person making rolls, and that we had to wait for the to go orders because they were concerned about not meeting the to go delivery deadlines. When we asked about "but what about the people that are actually at your restaurant?" we were met with a shrug and told to wait another 15 minutes.

About 25 minutes after that, when my mom went in to ask what was going on, she was rudely told she needed to be patient and that this "isn't fast food"

Such high hopes for this fun menu, but unfortunately the lack of understanding in how to do table service, combined with the rude dismissal of our concerns will keep us from ever going back or suggesting it to anybody.<//Text>

<UserId.>103013229929186729434< /UserId.>< Name>
Daria Fluor<//Name>
<time>1578948270324</time><rate>4<//rate>< review>
Great spot for cocktails. I've been here a few times and have never been disappointed by my selection. It does rotate somewhat seasonally, which is always nice.

It's got a great vibe with impeccable decorations, blending in nicely with its setting of the lobby of an old financial building. I only take a star off because it's not a really a destination for more than one drink. It is SUPER popular for a post-work drink, where you will have a hard time finding a spot to sit and it's quite loud (though honestly this is true for most bars in the immediate area). I've also gone after dinner, and this is truly the best time to go if you want a more chill vibe. Unfortunately because of the location, last call is about 10 PM or so - once again really only able to enjoy one drink.

If you're looking for an early-night cap, this is your spot!< /review>

Sadly, I have to give a low rating for this salon. I went for a full set as a walk-in and was told the wait was 2hrs. So it's not really a great place for a walk-in - make an appointment. (Especially if you have a 20 min drive to get there.) Even after we came back for our appt 2 hrs later, we ended up waiting another 30-40 min to get to a station. Once I sat down, my dude came up to the station an then left for about 10 minutes. He was super friendly and when I told him I wanted acrylics, he pushed the dip method on me pretty hard. I said OK and went with it. One of the colors I picked they didn't have. My nail shape (almond) and length ended up perfect, but the roundness of my nails are funky - almost looking pregnant if you look at them horizontally. (That's the only way I can describe). You can't really tell unless you really analyze them. But overall they look OK. Two weeks and no lifting, but if I run my fingers through my hair, the hair catches on the back of the nails where they've grown away from the cuticles. I bet if I messed with them at that spot, they'd come off pretty easily.

The salon doesn't look very clean and they were pretty scattered. One of the girls there kept poking or tickling my nail dude and did it once when he had the metal electric file on my hands which freaked me out. Those hurt when they touch skin!!

Prices are OK - about average for nail salons in the valley. My friend that went with me was given to a tech that we were told was there on his first day and they didn't seem too confident in his work and told us the first client he had hated his work. He did a nice job though considering she wanted a black to hot pink ombre color.

I may go back for maybe just a pedicure - but they definitely need to clean the place up and get a better rhythm there for me to update my rating.</text>

BUT I do wish they were a little more organized on the administrative side -- it is always nerve-wracking when they are not sure what your insurance is going to cover, or give you a referral to a specialist or tech who does NOT accept your insurance, or when you don't receive any bills (by letter OR email) for months and months and then find out you have an outstanding balance at your next ANNUAL exam. These are not all my own personal experiences; some are the experiences of my friends and colleagues who also use this clinic, but they have happened repeatedly... Ultimately, these things turn out okay because my friends and I are privileged/fortunate enough that an unexpected $30 or $50 charge doesn't destroy our finances. But it can add up, and not everyone is in that situation.

All-in-all, Rose Women's Health does the most important things 100% right: quality medical care, clear medical information and instructions, compassion and thoughtfulness. It's just the billing and handling of insurance that is a little vexing.</Text>

< review>
I was extremely impressed with Nurse Practitioner Jennifer Li.  I was looking for a new gynecologist and was told Dr. Rose is excellent. But, when I tried to make an appointment,  I found she was not accepting new patients. That's a good sign as she is busy and her waiting room had many pregnant women who looked very happy to be there.

A friend suggested that since I just wanted an annual check up that I should make my appointment with Jennifer Li, a Nurse Practitioner in Dr. Rose's office. I had never considered going to a Nurse Practitioner before, but my friend recommended her so extremely highly,  I decided to make my appointment with Jennifer.

Yesterday was my appointment and I have to say, I LOVE Jennifer Li. She is adorable, extremely friendly, made me feel totally at ease which is saying something when you are in the stirrups, and she was completely upbeat and made me feel she was very pleased to have met me. She was efficient and explained everything she was doing. It almost made having a pelvic exam a delight just to be around her cheerful personality.

When I got home, I told my husband that I sure wish Jennifer were around 30+ years ago when we were having our kids. I would have loved to go to her for my monthly check ups.

So, if you are debating as to whether to use a Nurse Practitioner, have no fear with Jennifer Li.  I know you will like her as much as I do.< /review>

< text>
My previous Dr dismissed my symptoms and even dared to say that I was crazy.
In an act of desperation, I yelped top OBGYN in Arcadia and Dr Rose topped the chart, I scheduled an appointment knowing that my consultations would be out of pocket because she was out of network.
Money Well Spent -under score-
On my first visit, she immediately ordered several tests and by my second visit she told me what was wrong with me. Turns out I was not ‚Äúcrazy‚Äù.
Dr Rose performed a total histerectomy on Feb 16,2018. She was at the pre-op unit on time, she spoke to me before the operation and when in the operating room we talked some more until the anesthesia took effect. Her down to earth caring demeaner, put any nerveousness I might have felt at ease. I knew I was in excellent hands.
Dr Rose checked on me the two days I was hospitalized, her visits where not rushed, she made sure to check my incision and answered any questions I had.
I am finally on the road to much better health thanks to Dr Rose.
Therefore, Based in my personal experience with Dr Rose, it makes me wish more doctors had the same level of professionalism, care & humanity as she does. I cannot praise her and her staff (specially Nicole) enough.
I highly recommend her.</text>
